IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND [o].[object_id] NOT IN (SELECT [ep].[major_id]
        FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
        WHERE [ep].[minor_id] = 0
            AND [ep].[class] = 1
            AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
